#### Formation of the 1st Tank Corps ####
country_event = {

	id = 500320
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	title = "1st Tank Corps"
	desc = "EVTDESC500320"
	picture = "TankCorps1"

	option = {
		name = "Form the 1st Tank Corps"
		set_country_flag = 1st_TC
		supplies = -1000
		manpower = -10
		metal = -500

		remove_brigade = "HQ 1-iy Mechanizirovanniy Korpus"
		remove_brigade = "1-ya Tankovaja Divizija"
		remove_brigade = "3-ya Tankovaja Divizija"
		remove_brigade = "3-ya Tankovaja Divizija/II"
		remove_brigade = "163-iy Mechanizirovanniy Divizija"
		remove_brigade = "1st Mechanised Corps Divisional Support"
		remove_brigade = "5-iy Mototsikl-Razvedchik Polk"
		remove_brigade = "Transport-Company 1st Mechanised Corps"
		
		clr_country_flag = 1stMechold
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
        OMG = {
            any_country = {
                limit = { tag = SOV has_country_flag = BlackICE
                    check_variable = { which = "BaseIC" value = 1 }
                    not = { check_variable = { which = "BaseIC" value = 150 } }               
                }
                add_country_modifier = {
                    name = "20IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_125_I"
                    duration = 90
                }	
                load_oob = SOV/SOV_1st_tankcorps43jan_build.txt
            }
        }
        OMG = {
            any_country = {
                limit = { tag = SOV has_country_flag = BlackICE
                    check_variable = { which = "BaseIC" value = 150 }
                    not = { check_variable = { which = "BaseIC" value = 200 } }
                }
                add_country_modifier = {
                    name = "20IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_150_I"
                    duration = 90
                }	
                load_oob = SOV/SOV_1st_tankcorps43jan_build.txt

        }
        OMG = {

                    name = "20IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_250_I"

                    duration = 90
                }	
                load_oob = SOV/SOV_1st_tankcorps43jan_build.txt
            }
        }
		
		OMG = {			#AI
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = SOV NOT = { has_country_flag = BlackICE } }
				load_oob = SOV/SOV_1st_tankcorps43jan.txt
			}
		}

	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no
		set_country_flag = 1st_TC
		clr_country_flag = 1stMechold
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

#### 1st Tank Corps 1943 upgrade ####
country_event = {

	id = 500321
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	title = "1st Tank Corps upgrade"
	desc = "EVTDESC500321"
	picture = "TankCorps1"

	option = {
		name = "Refit the 1st Tank Corps"
		set_country_flag = 1st_TC_upgrade
		supplies = -1000
		manpower = -5
		metal = -500
		
		remove_brigade = "HQ 1st Tank Corps"
		remove_brigade = "89/117/159th Tank Brigades"
		remove_brigade = "44th Motorised Rifle Brigade"
		remove_brigade = "Divisional Support 1st Tank Corps"
		remove_brigade = "Motorcycle Recon Battalion 1st Tank Corps"
		remove_brigade = "Transport-Bat. 1st Tank Corps"
		
		clr_country_flag = 1st_TC
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
        OMG = {
            any_country = {
                limit = { tag = SOV has_country_flag = BlackICE
                        check_variable = { which = "BaseIC" value = 1 }
                        not = { check_variable = { which = "BaseIC" value = 150 } }
                }
                add_country_modifier = {
                    name = "25IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_125_I"
                    duration = 90
                }

#### 12th Tank Corps upgrade to 6th Guards Tank Corps ####

	id = 500347

	desc = "EVTDESC500347"
	picture = "GuardTankCorps2"

		metal = -500

        OMG = {
            any_country = {
                limit = { tag = SOV has_country_flag = BlackICE

#### 6th Mechanised Corps upgrade to 5th Guards Mechanised Corps ####
country_event = {

	id = 500354
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	title = "5th Guards Mechanised Corps"
	desc = "EVTDESC500354"
	picture = "GuardMechCorps1"

	option = {
		name = "Grant Guard status to the 6th Mechanised Corps"
		set_country_flag = 5th_Guards_MC
		supplies = -1000
		manpower = -5
		metal = -500
		
		remove_brigade = "HQ 6th Mechanised Corps"
		remove_brigade = "50/54th Mechanised Brigades"
		remove_brigade = "162nd/163rd Separate Tank Regiments"
		remove_brigade = "Divisional Support 6th Mechanised Corps"
		remove_brigade = "Engineer-Bat. 6th Mechanised Corps"
		remove_brigade = "Motorcycle Recon Bat. 6th Mechanised Corps"
		remove_brigade = "Transport-Bat. 6th Mechanised Corps"
		
		clr_country_flag = 6th_MC
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
		OMG = {			#PLAYER
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = SOV has_country_flag = BlackICE }
				load_oob = SOV_5th_guards_mechcorps_uild.txt
			}
		}
		
		OMG = {			#AI
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = SOV NOT = { has_country_flag = BlackICE } }
				load_oob = SOV/SOV_5th_guards_mechcorps.txt
			}
		}

	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no
		set_country_flag = 5th_Guards_MC
		clr_country_flag = 6th_MC
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

### Allow formation and upgrades of Soviet Mechanised and Tank corps
country_event = {

	id = 500406
		
	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		year = 1936
		not = { has_country_flag = upgrades_yes }
		not = { has_country_flag = upgrades_no }
	}
	
	title = "Red Army Mechanised and Tank Corps Upgrade Events"
	desc = "EVTDESC500406"
	picture = "EarlyTank2"

	
	option = {
		name = "Allow the events" # ok
		set_country_flag = upgrades_yes
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Thanks"  # no
		set_country_flag = upgrades_no
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}
